line-height: 1.5;"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal *:first:mt-0 *:last:mb-0"><p>Done. The script now performs the split itself — no manual <code class="">Ctrl+D</code>.</p>
<p>What it does:</p>
<ol class="list-inside list-decimal whitespace-normal [li_&amp;]:pl-6" data-streamdown="ordered-list">
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">Clicks <code class="">button[aria-label="Chat actions"]</code> (the "…" menu).</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">Opens the <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Split</span> submenu (via pointer/hover events) and clicks <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Right</span>.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">Waits for the new tile to mount and targets it (last tile).</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">Sets that tile's model to <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Auto</span>.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">Types <code class="">PROMPT</code>, sends (mic-safe check), and <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">stops after 5s</span>.</li>
</ol>
<p>I also updated the note <code class="">Chat Automation - DevTools.md</code> — section <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">8.5</span> is now "Self-split (no manual Ctrl+D)" with the verified selectors (<code class="">[aria-label="Chat actions"]</code>, Split→Right portal items, model picker) and a caveat about radix submenu timing.</p>
<p>Key point: real menu <code class="">.click()</code>s work even though synthetic <code class="">Ctrl+D</code> keystrokes don't, so this replaces the manual hotkey entirely. If the <code class="">Right</code> item ever isn't found, bump the <code class="">sleep(300)</code> after hovering Split, or verify the menu text hasn't changed.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-flat-index="55" style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 6px;"><div tabindex="0" data-message-index="55"
